This summary of the calculated values for the transport block size can be printed out by setting the flags
**.useExtendedMcsTable = true
**.printTBS = true
in the ini-file (the function calcTBS in the LteMCS.cc file is called with different number of resource blocks). 
All values were checked via the site https://5g-tools.com/5g-nr-tbs-transport-block-size-calculator/
(with the following values, which are set by default in the simulator:
Number of scheduled OFDM symbols: 14
Number of RE for DMRS per PRB: 12
Overhead configured by higher layer: 0
)
